   var showOverlib;
   function popScreenshot(games_id, width, height) {
      features = 'status=no,resizable=no,menubar=no,titlebar=no,location=no,hotkeys=no,width=' + width + ',height=' + height;
      window.open('screenshot.php?games_id=' + games_id, 'SCREENSHOT', features);
   }

   function saveScreenshot(games_id, width, height) {
      features = 'status=no,resizable=no,menubar=no,titlebar=no,location=no,hotkeys=no,width=' + width + ',height=' + height;
      window.open('screenshot.php?save=1&games_id=' + games_id, 'SCREENSHOT', features);
   }
   function move_check(query, url) {
      var reply = confirm(query);
      if (reply) {
         this.location.href = url;
      }
   }

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var grantVisionMenu = document.getElementById('grant-vision-menu');
    var grantVisionMenuToggle = document.getElementById('grant-vision-menu-toggle');
    var m_table = document.getElementById("game-map-menu-dropdown");
    var p_table = document.getElementById("showinfo");
    var v_table = document.getElementById("showview");
    var p_td = document.getElementById("game_info");
    var v_td = document.getElementById("view_settings");
    
    function ToggleMenu() {
      if (m_table.style.display === "none") {
        m_table.style.display = "block";
        p_table.style.display = "none";
        v_table.style.display = "none";

      }
        
      else {
        m_table.style.display = "none";
        p_table.style.display = "none";
        v_table.style.display = "none";

        if(grantVisionMenu && grantVisionMenuToggle) {
          grantVisionMenu.style.display = 'none';
        }
      }
    }

    function ToggleInfo() {
      if (p_table.style.display === "none") {
        p_table.style.display = "block";
        v_table.style.display = "none";

        if(grantVisionMenu && grantVisionMenuToggle) {
          grantVisionMenu.style.display = 'none';
        }
      }
      
      else {
        p_table.style.display = "none";
      }
    }

    function ToggleView() {
      if (v_table.style.display === "none") {
        v_table.style.display = "block";
        p_table.style.display = "none";

        if(grantVisionMenu && grantVisionMenuToggle) {
          grantVisionMenu.style.display = 'none';
        }
      }
        
      else {
          v_table.style.display = "none";
      }
    }

    //Grant vision options
    if(grantVisionMenuToggle) {
      const addFriendSelector = document.getElementById("grant-vision-selector");
      const grantVisionSelect = document.getElementById("grant-vision-select");
      const grantVisionBtn = document.getElementById("grant-vision-btn");
      const grantVisionMsg = document.getElementById("grant-vision-msg");
      const removeVisionBtn = document.getElementById("remove-vision-btn");
      const removeFriendSelector = document.getElementById("remove-vision-selector");
      const confirmGrantMenu = document.getElementById("grant-vision-confirmation");
      const confirmGrant = document.getElementById("grant-confirm");
      const confirmScreenFriend = document.getElementById("grant-vision-conf-friend");
      const grantCancel = document.getElementById("grant-cancel");

      grantVisionMenuToggle.onclick = function() {
        const menuDisplay = grantVisionMenu.style.display;
        applyCSS(grantVisionMenu, {
          display: (function() {
            if(menuDisplay === "none") {
              return "flex";
            } else {
              return "none";
            }
          })()
        })
        applyCSS(v_table, {display: "none"});
        // applyCSS(l_table, {display: "none"});
        applyCSS(p_table, {display: "none"});
      }
      //Change to confirm screen
      grantVisionBtn.onclick = function() {
        changeMenus(grantVisionSelect, confirmGrantMenu);
        confirmScreenFriend.textContent = addFriendSelector.value;
      }
      //Add selected friend
      confirmGrant.onclick = function() {
        updateVisionList("add", addFriendSelector, removeFriendSelector);
        changeMenus(confirmGrantMenu, grantVisionSelect);
      }
      grantCancel.onclick = function() {
        changeMenus(confirmGrantMenu, grantVisionSelect);
      }
      if(removeVisionBtn) {
        removeVisionBtn.onclick = function() {
          if(removeFriendSelector.value) {
            updateVisionList("remove", removeFriendSelector, addFriendSelector);
          }
        }
      }
      function updateVisionList(action, selector, addToSelector) {
        const  friend = selector.value;
        const userInfo = {
          action: action,
          gamesId: 1113750,
          selectedFriend: friend
        }
        axios.post("api/game/grant_vision.php", userInfo)
        .then(function(res) {
          applyCSS(grantVisionMsg, {display: "block"});
          grantVisionMsg.textContent = res.data;
          const friendOption = document.querySelector("#" + selector.id + " option[value='" + friend + "']")
          addToSelector.appendChild(friendOption);
        })
        .catch(function(err) {
          grantVisionMsg.textContent = err;
        })
      }
      function changeMenus(invisible, visible) {
        applyCSS(invisible, {display: "none"});
        applyCSS(visible, {display: "flex"});
      }
    }

</script>  </div>

<script>
  const shortcuts = {
    calculator: true,
    nextUnit: true
  }

  //game_shortcuts.js
  initializeShortcuts(shortcuts);

  //Hard refresh if user accesses page from history (back & forward arrows)

  function findStarValue(playerId) {
    const player = playersInfo[playerId];
    const playerSCOP = player.players_co_max_spower / 10;
    const coSCOP = player.co_max_spower / 10;
    const starValue = playerSCOP / coSCOP * 9000;
    return starValue;

      <!-- Script for the login box -->
      <script>
            var login = document.getElementById("login"),
                  formElements = [].slice.call(document.getElementsByClassName("login-input")),
                  loginForm = document.querySelector(".login-form"),
                  errSpan = document.getElementById("login-err"),
                  usernameInput = formElements[0],
                  passwordInput = formElements[1];
            var errMsg;

            var loginBox = document.querySelector("#login-tab");
            var forgotPassword = document.querySelector(".login-forgot-password");
            var forgotPasswordTab = document.querySelector("#forgot-password-tab");
            var forgotPasswordForm = document.querySelector(".forgot-password-form");

            var forgotPasswordSubmit = document.querySelector(".forgot-password-submit");
            var forgotPasswordRes = document.querySelector(".forgot-password-res");
            
            forgotPassword.onclick = function() {
                  toggleDisplays([
                        { el: loginBox, display: "none" }, 
                        { el: forgotPasswordTab, display: "block"}
                  ]);

                  var forgotPasswordBack = document.querySelector(".forgot-password-back");
                  forgotPasswordBack.onclick = function() {
                        //Reset to initial state
                        toggleDisplays([
                              { el: loginBox, display: "block" },
                              { el: forgotPasswordTab, display: "none" },
                              { el: forgotPasswordForm, display: "flex" },
                              { el: forgotPasswordRes, display: "none" }
                        ]);
                  }
            }

            forgotPasswordSubmit.onclick = function() {
                  var forgotPasswordUsername = document.querySelector(".forgot-password-username");
                  var forgotPasswordEmail = document.querySelector(".forgot-password-email");

                  axios.post("api/forgot_password.php", { 
                        username: forgotPasswordUsername.value,
                        email: forgotPasswordEmail.value 
                  })
                  .then(function(res) {

                        forgotPasswordRes.textContent = res.data.message;

                        toggleDisplays([
                              { el: forgotPasswordForm, display: "none" },
                              { el: forgotPasswordRes, display: "block" }
                        ]);
                  })
            }

            //Used for the login box's tabs
            function toggleDisplays(tabs) {
                  tabs.forEach(function(tab) { tab.el.style.display = tab.display });
            }
            
            login.onclick = function(e) {
                  e.preventDefault();
                  const uc = verifyEmpty(usernameInput),
                        pc = verifyEmpty(passwordInput);
                  if(uc && pc) {
                        formElements.forEach(function(el) {
                              el.style.background = "";
                        })
                        verifyLogin().done(function(match) {
                              //1 means match, 0 means no match
                              if(match == 0) { showErr(); }
                              else if(match == 1) { loginForm.submit(); loadCurrPage(); }
                        })
                  }
            }   
            function verifyEmpty(el) {
                  if(el.value.length === 0) {
                        showErr()
                        return false;
                  }
                  else return true;
            } 
            function verifyLogin() {
                  const post = $.post("logincheck.php", {username: usernameInput.value, password: passwordInput.value});
                  return post;
            }
            function showErr() {
                  var errMsg = "Username or Password is incorrect";
                  errSpan.textContent = errMsg;
            }
            function loadCurrPage() {
                  window.location = 'game.php?games_id=1113750';
                  return false;
            }
      </script>

      <script>
            const fixedHeader = document.getElementById("fixed-header-wrapper");
            let smallHeader = false;
            if(window.pageYOffset !== 0) {
                  fixedHeader.classList.add("header-small")
            }
            document.body.onscroll = function() {
                  if(window.pageYOffset !== 0 && smallHeader === false) {
                        // console.log("?");
                        smallHeader = true;
                        fixedHeader.classList.add("header-small");
                  } else if(window.pageYOffset === 0) {
                        smallHeader = false;
                        fixedHeader.classList.remove("header-small");
                  }
            }
            

      </script>
<script src="js/jquery-3.3.1.min.js"></script>
</body>
</html>
